//=======
// Allies
//=======

Actor MarineBulletPuff : ModdedBulletPuff Replaces ModdedBulletPuff
{
DamageType "Marine"
//Species "Player"
+MTHRUSPECIES
}

Actor LegMarineBulletPuff : LegendaryASGBulletPuff Replaces LegendaryASGBulletPuff
{
DamageType "Marine"
//Species "Player"
+MTHRUSPECIES
}

ACTOR MarineRailPuff : PlayerRailPuff replaces PlayerRailPuff{DamageType "Marine"}

Actor SentryGun
{
  Obituary "%o was ventilated by an auto-sentry."
  Health 300
  Radius 16
  Height 56
  Mass 100000
  Speed 0
  Monster
  MaxTargetRange 1024
  AttackSound "m60/fire"
  DeathSound "sentry/die"
  Decal "BulletChip"
  +FLOORCLIP
  +FRIENDLY
  +MISSILEMORE
  +MISSILEEVENMORE
  +QUICKTORETALIATE
  +NOBLOOD
  +LOOKALLAROUND
  +NEVERRESPAWN
  +NOBLOCKMONST
  +DROPOFF
  +STANDSTILL
  +DONTHARMSPECIES
  -SOLID
  -COUNTKILL
  DamageFactor "Marine", 0
  DamageFactor "MarinePierce", 0.0
  DamageFactor "MarineKaboom", 0.0
  DamageFactor "Legendary", 0
  DamageFactor "LegendaryGuruPlayer", 0
  DamageFactor "LegendaryGuru", 0
  DamageFactor "MechStep", 0
  DamageFactor "Mine", 0.0
  DamageFactor "DBFG2", 0.0
  RadiusDamageFactor 0.5
  Species "Player"
  var int user_delay;
  var int user_script;
  var int user_slot;
  var int user_player;
  Tag "\c[a6]UAC \c[v2]- \c[l2]Sentry Gun\c-"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_script == 1,3)
    TNT1 A 0 ACS_ExecuteAlways(3601,0,0,0,0)
    TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_script",1)
    SENT A 0 A_JumpIf(user_delay >= 65,"Done")
    SENT AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 4 A_LookEx(LOF_NOSOUNDCHECK|LOF_NOSEESOUND)
	SENT A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_delay",user_delay+1)
    SENT A 0 A_PlaySound("sentry/beep")
    Loop
  See:
    TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_script == 1,3)
    TNT1 A 0 ACS_ExecuteAlways(3601,0,0,0,0)
    TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_script",1)
    SENT A 0 A_JumpIf(user_delay >= 65,"Done")
    SENT AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_Chase
	SENT AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_Chase
	SENT AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_Chase
	SENT AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_Chase
	SENT A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_delay",user_delay+1)
    SENT A 0 A_PlaySound("sentry/beep")
	SENT A 0 A_ClearTarget
    Loop
  Missile:
    SENT A 0 A_PlaySound("sentry/see")
    SENT A 1 A_FaceTarget
	SENT B 0 A_CustomMissile("MonsterTracer",Random(38,42),0,Random(5,-5),0)
    SENT B 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RifleCasing", 12, 6, 30, Random(2, 6), 0, Random(1, 3), Random(-80, -90), 128)
    SENT B 1 Bright A_CustomBulletAttack(3,3,1,random(1,5)*3,"MarineBulletPuff")
	SENT B 0 A_Jump(16,"See")
    SENT B 1 A_CPosRefire
    Goto Missile+1
  Done:
    SENT AAA 35 A_PlaySound("sentry/warn")
	SENT A 1 A_Die
    Goto See
  Death:
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("OrangeParticleSpawner", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 128)
    TNT1 AAA 0 A_CustomMissile("Kaboom3", 0, 0, random(0,360), 2, random(0,360))
	TNT1 AAA 0 A_CustomMissile("SmokeFX2", 0, 0, random(0,360), 2, random(0,360))
    TNT1 AAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Debris",0,0,0,Random(4,-4),Random(4,-4),Random(4,8),0,128)
    TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/rocklx")
    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("RocketEx",0,32)
	SENT C 0 A_NoBlocking
	SENT C 0 A_Scream
    SENT C 250
    Stop
  }
}

Actor SentryGun2 : SentryGun
{
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    SENT A 0 A_JumpIf(user_delay >= 65,"Done")
    SENT AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 4 A_LookEx(LOF_NOSOUNDCHECK|LOF_NOSEESOUND)
	SENT A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_delay",user_delay+1)
    SENT A 0 A_PlaySound("sentry/beep")
    Loop
  See:
    SENT A 0 A_JumpIf(user_delay >= 65,"Done")
    SENT AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_Chase
	SENT AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_Chase
	SENT AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_Chase
	SENT AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_Chase
	SENT A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_delay",user_delay+1)
    SENT A 0 A_PlaySound("sentry/beep")
	SENT A 0 A_ClearTarget
    Loop
  }
}

Actor RangeSentryGun : SentryGun
{
  MaxTargetRange 2048
  Health 250
  AttackSound "weapons/arifle"
  Tag "\c[a6]UAC \c[v2]- \c[w3]Range Sentry Gun\c-"

  {

    TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_script",1)
    SET2 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_delay >= 65,"Done")

	SET2 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_delay",user_delay+1)
    SET2 A 0 A_PlaySound("sentry/beep")
    Loop
  See:
    TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_script == 1,3)

    TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_script",1)
    SET2 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_delay >= 65,"Done")
    SET2 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_Chase
	SET2 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_Chase
	SET2 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_Chase
	SET2 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_Chase
	SET2 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_delay",user_delay+1)
    SET2 A 0 A_PlaySound("sentry/beep")
	SET2 A 0 A_ClearTarget
    Loop
  Missile:

    SET2 B 2 Bright A_CustomBulletAttack(1,1,1,random(1,5)*2,"MarineBulletPuff")
	SET2 C 2 A_FaceTarget
    SET2 B 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RifleCasing", 12, 6, 30, Random(2, 6), 0, Random(1, 3), Random(-80, -90), 128)
    SET2 B 2 Bright A_CustomBulletAttack(1,1,1,random(1,5)*2,"MarineBulletPuff")

    SET2 B 2 Bright A_CustomBulletAttack(1,1,1,random(1,5)*2,"MarineBulletPuff")
	SET2 C 2 A_FaceTarget
	SET2 A 0 A_Jump(16,"See")
    SET2 A 1 A_CPosRefire
    Goto Missile+1
  Done:
    SET2 AAA 35 A_PlaySound("sentry/warn")
	SET2 A 1 A_Die
    Goto See
  }
}

Actor SniperSentryGun : SentryGun
{
  MaxTargetRange 3072
  AttackSound "sniper/fire"
  Tag "\c[a6]UAC \c[v2]- \c[m3]Sniper Sentry Gun\c-"

    TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_script",1)
    SET3 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_delay >= 65,"Done")
    SET3 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 4 A_LookEx(LOF_NOSOUNDCHECK|LOF_NOSEESOUND)
	SET3 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_delay",user_delay+1)
    SET3 A 0 A_PlaySound("sentry/beep")
    Loop
  See:
    TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_script == 1,3)

    TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_script",1)
    SET3 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_delay >= 65,"Done")
    SET3 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_Chase
	SET3 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_Chase

	SET3 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_delay",user_delay+1)
    SET3 A 0 A_PlaySound("sentry/beep")
	SET3 A 0 A_ClearTarget
    Loop
  Missile:

    SET3 AAA 4 A_FaceTarget

	SET3 CCAA 2 A_FaceTarget
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RifleCasing", 12, 6, 30, Random(2, 6), 0, Random(1, 3), Random(-80, -90), 128)
    SET3 A 10 A_PlaySound("sniper/clip")

  Done:

  }

Actor ShotgunSentryGun : SentryGun
{
  AttackSound ""
  Tag "\c[a6]UAC \c[v2]- \c[m6]Shotgun Sentry Gun\c-"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_script == 1,3)
    TNT1 A 0 ACS_ExecuteAlways(3601,0,0,0,0)
    TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_script",1)
    SET4 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_delay >= 65,"Done")
    SET4 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 4 A_LookEx(LOF_NOSOUNDCHECK|LOF_NOSEESOUND)
	SET4 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_delay",user_delay+1)
    SET4 A 0 A_PlaySound("sentry/beep")
    Loop
  See:
    TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_script == 1,3)
    TNT1 A 0 ACS_ExecuteAlways(3601,0,0,0,0)
    TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_script",1)
    SET4 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_delay >= 65,"Done")
    SET4 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_Chase
	SET4 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_Chase
	SET4 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_Chase
	SET4 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_Chase
	SET4 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_delay",user_delay+1)
    SET4 A 0 A_PlaySound("sentry/beep")
	SET4 A 0 A_ClearTarget
    Loop
  Missile:
    SET4 A 0 A_PlaySound("Turret/sight")
    SET4 A 1 A_Jump(256,"AssautShotgun","DoubleShotgun","QuadShotgun")
    Goto See
  AssautShotgun:
    SET4 A 5 A_FaceTarget
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("asg/fire")
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ShellCasing", -8, 7, 30, 4, 0, (0.1)*Random(30, 40), Random(-80, -90), 128)
	TNT1 AAAA 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("MonsterTracer2",Random(28,34),0,Random(6,-6),0)
    SET4 E 13 Bright A_CustomBulletAttack(22.5,0,5,4,"MarineBulletPuff")
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("asg/fire")
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ShellCasing", -8, 7, 30, 4, 0, (0.1)*Random(30, 40), Random(-80, -90), 128)
	TNT1 AAAA 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("MonsterTracer2",Random(28,34),0,Random(6,-6),0)
    SET4 F 13 Bright A_CustomBulletAttack(22.5,0,5,4,"MarineBulletPuff")
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("asg/fire")
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ShellCasing", -8, 7, 30, 4, 0, (0.1)*Random(30, 40), Random(-80, -90), 128)
	TNT1 AAAA 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("MonsterTracer2",Random(28,34),0,Random(6,-6),0)
    SET4 G 13 Bright A_CustomBulletAttack(22.5,0,5,4,"MarineBulletPuff")
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("asg/fire")
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ShellCasing", -8, 7, 30, 4, 0, (0.1)*Random(30, 40), Random(-80, -90), 128)
	TNT1 AAAA 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("MonsterTracer2",Random(28,34),0,Random(6,-6),0)
    SET4 H 13 Bright A_CustomBulletAttack(22.5,0,5,4,"MarineBulletPuff")
    SET4 A 6 A_CposRefire
    Goto Missile+1
  DoubleShotgun:
    SET4 A 5 A_FaceTarget
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/sshotf")
	TNT1 AAAAAAAA 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("MonsterTracer2",Random(28,34),0,Random(6,-6),0)
	SET4 B 5 Bright A_CustomBulletAttack(13.8,9.6,10,Random(1,4)*3,"MarineBulletPuff")
	SET4 A 15 A_FaceTarget
	SET4 A 6 A_PlaySound("weapons/sawedopen")
	SET4 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ShellCasing", -10, 6, 36, Random(2, 6), 0, Random(1, 3), Random(-80, -90), 128)
	SET4 A 1 A_SpawnItemEx("ShellCasing", -10, 6, 36, Random(2, 6), 0, Random(1, 3), Random(-80, -90), 128)
	SET4 A 6 A_PlaySound("weapons/shellslide")
	SET4 A 6 A_PlaySound("weapons/sawedclose")
	SET4 A 6 A_CposRefire
	Goto Missile+1
  QuadShotgun:
    SET4 A 5 A_FaceTarget
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/qsgfire")
	TNT1 AAAAAAAAAAAA 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("MonsterTracer2",Random(28,34),0,Random(6,-6),0)
	SET4 C 5 Bright A_CustomBulletAttack(15.4,10.6,24,Random(1,4)*3,"MarineBulletPuff")
	SET4 A 25 A_FaceTarget
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/qsgopen")
	SET4 A 15 A_FaceTarget
	SET4 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ShellCasing", -8, 6, 36, Random(2, 6), 0, Random(1, 3), Random(-80, -90), 128)
	SET4 A 1 A_SpawnItemEx("ShellCasing", -8, 6, 36, Random(2, 6), 0, Random(1, 3), Random(-80, -90), 128)
	SET4 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ShellCasing", -8, 6, 36, Random(2, 6), 0, Random(1, 3), Random(-80, -90), 128)
	SET4 A 2 A_SpawnItemEx("ShellCasing", -8, 6, 36, Random(2, 6), 0, Random(1, 3), Random(-80, -90), 128)
	SET4 A 12 A_PlaySound("weapons/qsgshellslide")
	SET4 A 8
	SET4 A 12 A_PlaySound("weapons/qsgshellslide")
	SET4 A 8
	SET4 A 10 A_PlaySound("weapons/qsgclose")
	SET4 A 2 A_CposRefire
	Goto Missile+1
  Done:
    SET4 AAA 35 A_PlaySound("sentry/warn")
	SET4 A 1 A_Die
    Goto See
  }
}

Actor FlameSentryGun : SentryGun
{
  MaxTargetRange 354
  Health 400
  AttackSound ""
  Tag "\c[a6]UAC \c[v2]- \c[z4]Flame Sentry Gun\c-"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_script == 1,3)
    TNT1 A 0 ACS_ExecuteAlways(3601,0,0,0,0)
    TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_script",1)
    SET5 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_delay >= 65,"Done")
    SET5 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 4 A_LookEx(LOF_NOSOUNDCHECK|LOF_NOSEESOUND)
	SET5 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_delay",user_delay+1)
    SET5 A 0 A_PlaySound("sentry/beep")
    Loop
  See:
    TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_script == 1,3)
    TNT1 A 0 ACS_ExecuteAlways(3601,0,0,0,0)
    TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_script",1)
    SET5 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_delay >= 65,"Done")
    SET5 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_Chase
	SET5 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_Chase
	SET5 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_Chase
	SET5 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_Chase
	SET5 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_delay",user_delay+1)
    SET5 A 0 A_PlaySound("sentry/beep")
	SET5 A 0 A_ClearTarget
    Loop
  Missile:
    SET5 A 0 A_PlaySound("sentry/see")
	SET5 A 1 A_JumpIfCloser(455,1)
	Goto See
    SET5 AA 2 A_FaceTarget
	SET5 A 3 A_PlayWeaponSound("hectebus/flameready")
	SET5 AA 4 A_FaceTarget
    SET5 B 0 A_PlaySound("monsters/fatsofire")
	SET5 B 3 Bright A_CustomMissile("SentryFlame",46,0,random(-1,1))
	SET5 A 2 A_FaceTarget
	SET5 B 3 Bright A_CustomMissile("SentryFlame",46,0,random(-1,1))
	SET5 A 2 A_FaceTarget
	SET5 B 3 Bright A_CustomMissile("SentryFlame",46,0,random(-1,1))
	SET5 A 2 A_FaceTarget
	SET5 B 3 Bright A_CustomMissile("SentryFlame",46,0,random(-1,1))
	SET5 A 2 A_FaceTarget
	SET5 B 3 Bright A_CustomMissile("SentryFlame",46,0,random(-1,1))
	SET5 A 2 A_FaceTarget
	SET5 B 3 Bright A_CustomMissile("SentryFlame",46,0,random(-1,1))
	SET5 A 2 A_FaceTarget
	SET5 B 3 Bright A_CustomMissile("SentryFlame",46,0,random(-1,1))
	SET5 A 2 A_FaceTarget
	SET5 B 3 Bright A_CustomMissile("SentryFlame",46,0,random(-1,1))
	SET5 A 2 A_FaceTarget
	SET5 B 3 Bright A_CustomMissile("SentryFlame",46,0,random(-1,1))
	SET5 A 2 A_FaceTarget
	SET5 A 4 A_CPosRefire
    Goto Missile+1
  Done:
    SET5 AAA 35 A_PlaySound("sentry/warn")
	SET5 A 1 A_Die
    Goto See
  }
}

ACTOR SentryFlame : PoisonSoulCloud
{
    Radius 10
    Height 10
	Scale 0.55
	Speed 14
	DamageType "Marine"
	Species "Player"
	PROJECTILE
	+THRUSPECIES
	-THRUACTORS
	-SKYEXPLODE
	Decal Scorch
    States
    {
    Spawn:
        FIR1 LKJIHGFEDCB 2 Bright A_Explode(5,68)
	Death:
		FIR1 AA 2 Bright A_FadeOut(0.25)
	    Stop
		}
}

Actor MiniRocket
{
Projectile
Damage 5
Height 5
Radius 6
Damagetype "Marine"
Speed 48
SeeSound ""
DeathSound "MiniRocketExpl"
Decal DoomImpScorch
States
{
Spawn:
	MICR A 1 Bright A_SpawnItemEx("MissileTrail",0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("MiniRocketFly",0,1.0,0)
	Loop
Death:
	TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("OrangeParticleSpawner", 0, 0, 1, 0, 0, 0, 0, 128)
	TNT1 AAAA 0 A_CustomMissile("Kaboom9", 0, 0, random(0,360), 2, random(0,360))
	TNT1 AAAA 0 A_CustomMissile("SmokeFX4", 0, 0, random(0,360), 2, random(0,360))
	TNT1 A 0 A_Explode(10,30)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SetTranslucent(0.85,1)
	H2BL JKLMN 4 Bright
	Stop
}
}

Actor HeavySentryGun : SentryGun
{
  Health 650
  MaxTargetRange 3072
  DamageFactor 0.75
  RadiusDamageFactor 0.8

    Goto Missile+2

	SENT C 0 A_Scream

    Stop

DeathSound "player/death"
ActiveSound "player/active"
Obituary "%o was killed by a marine."
Decal BulletChip
MinMissileChance 2
DamageFactor 0.55
RadiusDamageFactor 0.55
+NODROPOFF
+FRIENDLY
+QUICKTORETALIATE
+DONTHARMSPECIES
+MISSILEMORE
+MISSILEEVENMORE
+NOBLOCKMONST
+FLOORCLIP
States
{
  Death:
	PLA1 I 10 A_Scream
	PLA1 J 10 A_NoBlocking
	PLA1 KLM 10
	PLA1 N 250
	Stop
  XDeath:
	PLAY O 5
	PLAY P 5 A_XScream
	PLAY Q 0 A_SpawnItemEx("GibbedGenerator",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,128,0)
	PLAY Q 5 A_NoBlocking
	PLAY RSTUV 5
	PLAY W 250
	Stop
}
}

Actor MGrenade : ThrownGrenade
{
Damage (0)
Damagetype "Marine"
Obituary "%o was exploded by a zombie specops."
States
{
  Spawn:
	TNT1 A 0
	HGN1 A 3 A_StopSound
	HGN1 BCDEFGHABCDEFGHABCDEFGH 3
	Goto Death
  Death:
	TNT1 A 0 
	TNT1 A 0
	HGN1 H 1 Bright A_ChangeFlag(EXTREMEDEATH,1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_AlertMonsters
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/hgrenadeex",CHAN_BODY)
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("Explosion",CHAN_WEAPON)
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("FAREXPL",CHAN_VOICE)
	TNT1 A 0 Radius_Quake(2,24,0,15,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Explode(128,146)
	TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("DiggerExplosion",0,0,random(80,100),2,random(80,100))
    TNT1 AAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Debris",0,0,0,random(4,-4),random(4,-4),random(4,8),0,128)
	TNT1 A 1 A_SpawnItem("DiggerEx")
    Stop
}
}

Actor AIStrafing : CustomInventory
{
  +INVENTORY.QUIET
  +INVENTORY.UNDROPPABLE
  +INVENTORY.ALWAYSPICKUP
  +INVENTORY.AUTOACTIVATE
  +COUNTITEM
  Inventory.Amount 1
  Inventory.MaxAmount 0
  States
  {
  Pickup:
    NULL A 1
	NULL A 1 A_GiveInventory("AIJumping",1)
	NULL A 1 A_JumpIf(velx != 0 || vely != 0,2)
	NULL A 1 A_Jump(256,2)
	NULL A 1 A_Jump(235,5)
	NULL A 1 A_JumpIfInventory("StrafeSens",1,3)
	NULL A 1 A_GiveInventory("StrafeSens",1)
	NULL A 1 A_Jump(256,2)
	NULL A 1 A_TakeInventory("StrafeSens",1)
	NULL A 1 A_JumpIfInventory("StrafeSens",1,3)
	NULL A 1 ThrustThing(angle*256/360+38.7,5,0,0)
	NULL A 1 A_Jump(256,2)
	NULL A 1 ThrustThing(angle*256/360+38.7,-5,0,0)
    NULL A 1 A_FaceTarget
	NULL A 1 A_Jump(24,2)
	NULL A 1 A_JumpIfCloser(300,2)
	NULL A 1 A_Recoil(-1.5)
    Stop
	NULL A 1 A_Recoil(1.5)
    Stop
  }
}

ACTOR StrafeSens : Inventory{Inventory.MaxAmount 1}

ACTOR UACGuyAR : UACBaseMarine
{
	AttackSound "weapons/arifle"
    Tag "\c[a6]UAC \c[v2]Marine - \c[m3]Assault Rifle\c-"
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		PLAY A 10 A_Look
		Goto Idle
	See:
	    PLAY A 0 A_JumpIfTargetInLOS("Strafing")
        PLAY AABB 3 A_Chase
        TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Check For Master Player Calling Help",0,0,0,0)
	    TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(16,"GiveUp")
        TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("FootStep",0,0,0,0)
        PLAY CCDD 3 A_Chase
        TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("FootStep",0,0,0,0)
        Loop
	Strafing:
		PLAY A 0 A_SpawnItem("FootStep",0,0,0,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Chase("","Missile",CHF_DONTMOVE)
		PLAY A 3 A_GiveInventory("AIStrafing",1)
        TNT1 A 0 A_Chase("","Missile",CHF_DONTMOVE)
		PLAY A 3 A_GiveInventory("AIStrafing",1)
        TNT1 A 0 A_Chase("","Missile",CHF_DONTMOVE)
		PLAY B 3 A_GiveInventory("AIStrafing",1)
        TNT1 A 0 A_Chase("","Missile",CHF_DONTMOVE)
		PLAY B 3 A_GiveInventory("AIStrafing",1)
        TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Check For Master Player Calling Help",0,0,0,0)
		PLAY C 0 A_SpawnItem("FootStep",0,0,0,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Chase("","Missile",CHF_DONTMOVE)
        PLAY C 3 A_GiveInventory("AIStrafing",1)
        TNT1 A 0 A_Chase("","Missile",CHF_DONTMOVE)
        PLAY C 3 A_GiveInventory("AIStrafing",1)
        TNT1 A 0 A_Chase("","Missile",CHF_DONTMOVE)
        PLAY D 3 A_GiveInventory("AIStrafing",1)
        TNT1 A 0 A_Chase("","Missile",CHF_DONTMOVE)
        PLAY D 3 A_GiveInventory("AIStrafing",1)
		Goto See
	Idle:
	    PLAY A 0 A_Jump(48,"Find")
        TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Check For Master Player Calling Help",0,0,0,0)
		PLAY A 0 A_SpawnItem("FootStep",0,0,0,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_LookEx(LOF_NOSOUNDCHECK|LOF_NOSEESOUND)
		PLAY AABB 3 A_GiveInventory("AIPatroling",1)
		PLAY C 0 A_SpawnItem("FootStep",0,0,0,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_LookEx(LOF_NOSOUNDCHECK|LOF_NOSEESOUND)
        PLAY CCDD 3 A_GiveInventory("AIPatroling",1)
		Loop
	Find:
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_ExecuteAlways(8883,0,0,0,0)
        Goto Idle
	GiveUp:
	    PLA1 A 10 A_ClearTarget
	    Goto Idle
    Missile:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(45,"FragGrenade")
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(750,"Close")
    Far:
        PLAY EE 5 A_GiveInventory("AIStrafing",1)
        TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RifleCasing", 12, 6, 30, Random(2, 6), 0, Random(1, 3), Random(-80, -90), 128)
        PLAY F 2 Bright A_CustomBulletAttack(15.4,0,1,5,"MarineBulletPuff")
        PLAY E 2 A_GiveInventory("AIStrafing",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RifleCasing", 12, 6, 30, Random(2, 6), 0, Random(1, 3), Random(-80, -90), 128)
        PLAY F 2 Bright A_CustomBulletAttack(15.4,0,1,5,"MarineBulletPuff")
        PLAY E 2 A_GiveInventory("AIStrafing",1)
        TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RifleCasing", 12, 6, 30, Random(2, 6), 0, Random(1, 3), Random(-80, -90), 128)
        PLAY F 2 Bright A_CustomBulletAttack(15.4,0,1,5,"MarineBulletPuff")
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(16,"See")
        TNT1 A 0 A_CPosRefire
        PLAY EE 5 A_GiveInventory("AIStrafing",1)
        Goto Far+2
    Close:

        PLAY EE 5 A_GiveInventory("AIStrafing",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("AIStrafing",1)
        TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RifleCasing", 12, 6, 30, Random(2, 6), 0, Random(1, 3), Random(-80, -90), 128)
        PLAY F 2 Bright A_CustomBulletAttack(22.5,0,1,random(1,5)*3,"MarineBulletPuff")
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(16,"See")
        TNT1 A 0 A_CPosRefire
        PLAY E 3 A_GiveInventory("AIStrafing",1)
		Goto Close+2
	FragGrenade:
        PLA1 E 1 A_JumpIfCloser(1000,1)
		Goto Missile
		PLA1 E 0 A_JumpIfCloser(280,"Missile")
        PLA1 E 6 A_GiveInventory("AIStrafing",1)
        PLA1 EEE 4 A_GiveInventory("AIStrafing",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("AIStrafing",1)
        PLA1 E 6 A_CustomMissile("MGrenade",32,0,0,2,10)
		PLA1 E 1
		Goto See
	 Pain:
		PLAY G 3 A_GiveInventory("AIStrafing",1)
		PLAY G 3 A_Pain
		Goto See
	}
}

		PLA9 E 6 A_PlaySound("weapons/shellslide")
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("AIStrafing",1)
		PLA9 E 6 A_PlaySound("weapons/sawedclose")
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("AIStrafing",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(40,"See")
		PLA9 E 6 A_CPosRefire
		Goto Missile
	FragGrenade:
        PLA1 E 1 A_JumpIfCloser(1000,1)
		Goto Missile
		PLA1 E 0 A_JumpIfCloser(280,"Missile")

	}

ACTOR ScoutDrone
{
Obituary "%o was betrayed."
Monster
Health 50
Radius 12
Height 28
Mass 100
Speed 15
+FRIENDLY
+QUICKTORETALIATE
+LOOKALLAROUND
+NEVERRESPAWN
+MISSILEMORE
+MISSILEEVENMORE
+NOBLOCKMONST
+FLOAT
+NOGRAVITY
+NOBLOOD
+NOPAIN
-COUNTKILL
AttackSound ""
DeathSound ""
Decal "BulletChip"
DamageFactor "Marine", 0
DamageFactor "MarinePierce", 0.0
DamageFactor "MarineKaboom", 0.0
DamageFactor "Legendary", 0
DamageFactor "LegendaryGuruPlayer", 0
DamageFactor "LegendaryGuru", 0
DamageFactor "MechStep", 0
DamageFactor "Mine", 0
DamageFactor "DBFG2", 0.0
Species "Player"
SeeSound "drone/see"
DeathSound "drone/die"
ActiveSound "drone/act"
var int user_slot;
var int user_delay;
var int user_script;
Scale 0.6
Tag "\c[a6]UAC \c[v2]- \c[m3]Scout Drone\c-"
States
{
  Spawn:
    DRON A 4 A_Look
    Goto See
  See:
    DRON A 0 A_JumpIf(user_delay >= 1700,"Done")
    DRON A 2 A_Chase
	DRON A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_delay",user_delay+1)
    Loop
  Missile:
    DRON A 0 A_JumpIf(user_delay >= 1700,"Done")
    DRON BBBB 2 A_FaceTarget
    DRON C 0 A_PlaySound("drone/fire")
    DRON C 3 Bright A_CustomMissile("DroneProj",15,0,random(-3,3))
	DRON C 0 A_PlaySound("drone/fire")
	DRON C 3 Bright A_CustomMissile("DroneProj",15,0,random(-3,3))
	DRON C 0 A_PlaySound("drone/fire")
	DRON C 3 Bright A_CustomMissile("DroneProj",15,0,random(-3,3))
    Goto See
  Done:
    DRON AAA 35 A_PlaySound("sentry/warn")
	DRON A 1 A_Die
    Goto See
  Death:
    DRON D 7 A_NoBlocking
    DRON E 8 A_Scream
    DRON F 5 A_Gravity
    Wait
  Crash:
    DRON GHI 4
	DRON J 250
    Stop
    }
}

ACTOR UACSentinel : ScoutDrone
{

+DONTFALL

{
  Spawn:
    TNT1 A 0 
    TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_script == 1,3)
    TNT1 A 0 ACS_ExecuteAlways(3601,0,0,0,0)
    TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_script",1)
    R0BS A 4 A_Look
	Goto Idle
  See:
    R0BS A 0 A_JumpIf(user_delay >= 5000,"Done")
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(4,"GiveUp")

    TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Check For Master Player Calling Help",0,0,0,0)
    R0BS DDEEFF 2 A_Chase
    Loop
  GiveUp:
	R0BS A 35 A_ClearTarget
	Goto Idle
  Idle:
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(8,"Find")
	TNT1 A 0 A_LookEx(LOF_NOSOUNDCHECK)
    R0BS AABBCC 2 A_Wander
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Check For Master Player Calling Help",0,0,0,0)
    R0BS DDEEFF 2 A_Wander
	Loop
  Find:
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_ExecuteAlways(8883,0,0,0,0)
	Goto Idle
  Missile:
    TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_delay >= 5000,"Done")
    R0BS AAAA 2 A_FaceTarget
    R0BS A 0 A_PlayWeaponSound("lrball3/shot")
    R0BS A 3 Bright A_CustomMissile("BattledroneElementalProjectile",54,0,0)
    R0BS AAAA 2 A_FaceTarget
    R0BS A 0 A_PlayWeaponSound("lrball3/shot")
    R0BS A 3 Bright A_CustomMissile("BattledroneElementalProjectile",54,0,0)
    R0BS AAAA 2 A_FaceTarget
    R0BS A 0 A_PlayWeaponSound("lrball3/shot")
    R0BS A 3 Bright A_CustomMissile("BattledroneElementalProjectile",54,0,0)
    R0BS AAAA 2 A_FaceTarget
    Goto See
  Done:
    R0BS AAA 35 A_PlaySound("sentry/warn")
	R0BS A 1 A_Die
    Goto See
  Death:
	TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 A_ScreamAndUnblock
	TNT1 A 0 A_KillChildren
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("OrangeParticleSpawner",0,0,32,0,0,0,0,128)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Debris",0,0,0,random(4,-4),random(4,-4),32,0,128)

	R0BS HIJK 5 Bright
	Stop
}

    TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_nomaster == 1,"Search")
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_ExecuteAlways(8883,0,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfTracerCloser(100,"Protect")
	TNT1 A 0 A_Stop
	TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTracer
	TNT1 A 0 A_Recoil(-21)
	RPBT A 0 A_RadiusGive("AdvancedRepairDroneRadiusGiverEffect",512,RGF_GIVESELF|RGF_MONSTERS,1)
	RPBT B 4 A_Chase("","Missile",CHF_DONTMOVE)
	RPBT A 0 A_JumpIfTracerCloser(150,"Protect")
    RPBT A 0 A_JumpIf(velx != 0 || vely != 0,2)
	RPBT A 0 A_Jump(256,"Search")
	RPBT A 0 A_Stop
	RPBT A 0 A_FaceTracer
	RPBT A 0 A_Recoil(-21)
	RPBT A 0 A_RadiusGive("AdvancedRepairDroneRadiusGiverEffect",512,RGF_GIVESELF|RGF_MONSTERS,1)
	RPBT B 4 A_Chase("","Missile",CHF_DONTMOVE)
	RPBT A 0 A_JumpIfTracerCloser(150,"Protect")
	RPBT A 0 A_Stop
	RPBT A 0 A_FaceTracer
	RPBT A 0 A_Recoil(-21)
	RPBT A 0 A_RadiusGive("AdvancedRepairDroneRadiusGiverEffect",512,RGF_GIVESELF|RGF_MONSTERS,1)
	RPBT B 4 A_Chase("","Missile",CHF_DONTMOVE)
	RPBT A 0 A_JumpIfTracerCloser(150,"Protect")
	RPBT A 0 A_Stop
	RPBT A 0 A_FaceTracer
	RPBT A 0 A_Recoil(-21)
	RPBT A 0 A_RadiusGive("AdvancedRepairDroneRadiusGiverEffect",512,RGF_GIVESELF|RGF_MONSTERS,1)
	RPBT B 4 A_Chase("","Missile",CHF_DONTMOVE)
    Loop
  Protect:
	RPBT A 0 A_Stop
	RPBT A 0 A_ClearTarget
	RPBT A 0 A_SetAngle(random(0,359))
	RPBT B 4 A_Chase("","Missile",CHF_DONTMOVE)
	RPBT A 0 A_RadiusGive("AdvancedRepairDroneRadiusGiverEffect",512,RGF_GIVESELF|RGF_MONSTERS,1)
	RPBT B 4 A_JumpIfTracerCloser(200,1)
	Goto See
	RPBT B 1 A_Jump(8,"Protect")
	Goto Protect+3
  Search:
    RPBT B 0 A_Jump(32,"Find")
	RPBT BBBBBBBBBBBBBBBBBBBBBBBBBBBB 2 A_Chase
    Goto See
  Find:
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_ExecuteAlways(8883,0,0,0,0)
    Goto See
  Missile:
	TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("MiniRocket",35,-4,random(-2,2))
	TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("MiniRocket",36,4,random(-2,2))
    RPBT C 2 Bright HealThing(1)
    Goto See
  Death:
	TNT1 A 0 
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/rocklx")
	TNT1 A 0 A_KillChildren
	TNT1 A 0 A_ScreamAndUnblock
	TNT1 AAAAAAAAA 0 A_CustomMissile("Kaboom", random(20,80), random(20,-20), random(0,360), 2, random(0,360))
	RPBT A 1 A_Gravity
	wait
  Crash:
	TNT1 AAAAAAA 0 A_CustomMissile("Kaboom", random(20,80), random(20,-20), random(0,360), 2, random(0,360))
	TNT1 AA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Debris",0,0,0,Random(4,-4),Random(4,-4),Random(4,8),0,128)
	RPBT Z 250
	Stop
}

	TNT1 AAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UtilityActorSlot",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_slot",1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(4,"GiveUp")
	FABN A 2 A_Chase
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,"Evade")
	FABN AAAA 2 A_Chase
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_battledroned1 >= 6,2)
	FABN A 0 A_Jump(48,"BuildDroneD1")
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_scoutdrone >= 15,2)
	FABN A 0 A_Jump(64,"BuildScoutDrone")
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Check For Master Player Calling Help",0,0,0,0)
	FABN AAAA 2 A_Chase
	Loop
  GiveUp:
	FABN A 35 A_ClearTarget
	Goto Idle
  Idle:
	FABN A 0 A_Jump(8,"Find")
	FABN A 0 A_LookEx(LOF_NOSOUNDCHECK)
	FABN AAAA 2 A_Wander
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_battledroned1 >= 6,2)
	FABN A 0 A_Jump(48,"BuildDroneD1")
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_scoutdrone >= 15,2)
	FABN A 0 A_Jump(64,"BuildScoutDrone")
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Check For Master Player Calling Help",0,0,0,0)
	FABN AAAA 2 A_Wander
	Loop
  Find:
	FABN A 0 ACS_ExecuteAlways(8883,0,0,0,0)
	Goto Idle
  Evade:
	FABN A 0 A_Jump(128,7)
	FABN A 0 ThrustThing(Angle*256/360+64,14,0,0)
	FABN AAAA 3 A_Chase
	FABN A 0 A_Stop
	Goto See
	FABN A 0 ThrustThing(Angle*256/360+192,14,0,0)
	FABN AAAA 3 A_Chase
	FABN A 0 A_Stop
	Goto See
  BuildScoutDrone:
	FABN BCD 4 A_FaceTarget
	FABN EFEFEFEF 3 Bright A_SpawnItemEx("ScoutDroneMarker",64,0,32)
	FABN A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scoutdrone",user_scoutdrone+1)
	FABN D 6 A_SpawnItemEx("ScoutDrone",64,0,32,0,0,0,0,32)
	FABN CB 2 A_FaceTarget
	Goto See
  BuildDroneD1:
    FABN BCD 4 A_FaceTarget
    FABN EFEFEFEF 3 Bright A_SpawnItemEx("BattleDroneD1Marker",64,0,32)
    FABN A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_battledroned1",user_battledroned1+1)
    FABN D 6 A_SpawnItemEx("BattleDroneD1v2",64,0,32,0,0,0,0,32)
	FABN CB 2 A_FaceTarget
	Goto See
  Missile:
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_battledroned1 >= 6,2)
	FABN A 0 A_Jump(128,"BuildDroneD1")
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_scoutdrone >= 15,2)
	FABN A 0 A_Jump(192,"BuildScoutDrone")
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlayWeaponSound("FocusedPlasma/Spin")
	FABN DDDDDDDDDD 3 A_GiveInventory("BattleDroneStrafe",1)
  Normal:
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("BattleDroneStrafe",1)
	FABN EF 2 Bright A_CustomMissile("FocusedPlasma",32,0,random(-8,8))
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(8,"SpinDown")
	TNT1 A 0 A_MonsterRefire(36,"SpinDown")
	Loop
  SpinDown:
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlayWeaponSound("FocusedPlasma/Down")
	FABN DDCBA 3
	Goto See
  Melee:
	FABN DDDDDDDDDD 3 A_FaceTarget
    Goto Normal
  Death:
	FABN A 0 A_PlaySound ("weapons/rocklx")
	FABN A 0 A_KillChildren
	FABN AAAAAAAAAA 0 A_CustomMissile("Kaboom", random(20,80), random(20,-20), random(0,360), 2, random(0,360))
	FABN A 0 A_NoBlocking
	FABN A 0 A_Scream
	FABN A 5 A_Gravity
	Wait
  Crash:
	FABN AAAAAAA 0 A_CustomMissile("Kaboom", random(20,80), random(20,-20), random(0,360), 2, random(0,360))
	FABN AA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Debris",0,0,0,Random(4,-4),Random(4,-4),Random(4,8),0,128)
	FABN Z 250
	Stop
}
}

  See:

	RLRD AABBCCDDEEFF 3 A_Chase("Melee","")
	TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_delay",user_delay+1)
	Loop
  Charge:

    RLRD A 2 A_Recoil(-1.6)

    RLRD B 2 A_Recoil(-1.6)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Chase("Melee","",CHF_DONTMOVE)

    RLRD D 2 A_Recoil(-1.6)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Chase("Melee","",CHF_DONTMOVE)
	TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget
    RLRD E 2 A_Recoil(-1.6)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Chase("Melee","",CHF_DONTMOVE)
	TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget
    RLRD F 2 A_Recoil(-1.6)
	Goto See
  Clear:
	TNT1 A 0 
	TNT1 A 0 ThrustThingZ(0,25,0,1)
	TNT1 A 0 ThrustThing(random(0,359),-8,0,0)
	RLRD A 1 A_ClearTarget
	Goto Spawn
  Melee:
	RLRD GHIJ 6 Bright
	TNT1 A 0 A_Die
	Goto See
  Done:
	RLRD GHIJ 6 Bright
    RLRD JJJJ 35 Bright A_PlaySound("sentry/warn")
	RLRD J 1 Bright A_Die
    Goto See
  Death:
	TNT1 A 0 A_ScreamAndUnblock
    TNT1 A 0 A_Explode(156,138)
    TNT1 AAA 0 A_CustomMissile("Kaboom3",0,0,random(0,360),2,random(0,360))
	TNT1 AAA 0 A_CustomMissile("SmokeFX2",0,0,random(0,360),2,random(0,360))

DamageFactor "MechStep", 0
DamageFactor "Mine", 0
DamageFactor "DBFG2", 0
DamageFactor 0.5
RadiusDamageFactor 0.5
MaxDropOffHeight 32
MaxStepHeight 32
Species "Player"
var int user_slot;
var int user_script;
SeeSound "b1battlebot/see"
ActiveSound "b1battlebot/idle"
DeathSound "b1battlebot/death"
Tag "\c[a6]UAC \c[v2]- \c[m3]Battle Bot B1\c-"
Decal BulletChip
States
{

  Spawn:
	TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_script",1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_slot",1)
	BTB1 A 2 A_Look
	Goto See
  See:
    TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_script == 1,3)
    TNT1 A 0 ACS_ExecuteAlways(3601,0,0,0,0)
    TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_script",1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(16,"GiveUp")
    BTB1 B 0 A_PlaySound("b1battlebot/step")
    BTB1 BBCC 3 A_Chase
    TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Check For Master Player Calling Help",0,0,0,0)
    BTB1 D 0 A_PlaySound("b1battlebot/step")
    BTB1 DDEE 3 A_Chase
    Goto See
  GiveUp:
	BTB1 A 35 A_ClearTarget
	Goto Idle
  Idle:
    TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(48,"Find")
	TNT1 A 0 A_LookEx(LOF_NOSOUNDCHECK)
	BTB1 B 0 A_PlaySound("b1battlebot/step")
    BTB1 BBCC 3 A_Wander
    TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Check For Master Player Calling Help",0,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_LookEx(LOF_NOSOUNDCHECK)
    BTB1 D 0 A_PlaySound("b1battlebot/step")
    BTB1 DDEE 3 A_Wander
	Loop
  Find:
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_ExecuteAlways(8883,0,0,0,0)
    Goto Idle
  Melee:
    BTB1 H 6 A_FaceTarget
    BTB1 I 7 A_CustomMeleeAttack(random(20,45),"b1battlebot/melee",none,"Marine")
    BTB1 H 7
    Goto See
  Missile:
    BTB1 F 1 A_Jump(140,"Missile2","Missile3","Missile4")
    BTB1 G 6 A_FaceTarget
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlayWeaponSound("AShotgun/Fire")
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ShellCasing", -8, 7, 30, 4, 0, (0.1)*Random(30, 40), Random(-80, -90), 128)
	TNT1 AAAA 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("MonsterTracer2",Random(28,34),0,Random(6,-6),0)
    BTB1 F 8 Bright A_CustomBulletAttack(22.5,0,5,4,"MarineBulletPuff")
    TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(50,"See")
    BTB1 F 1 Bright A_CPosRefire
    Goto Missile+1
  Missile2:
    BTB1 G 8 A_FaceTarget
    BTB1 F 0 A_CustomMissile("MiniRocket",32,4,0)
    BTB1 F 7 Bright A_CustomMissile("MiniRocket",32,-4,0)
    BTB1 F 1 Bright A_Jump(86,"Missile3")
    Goto See
  Missile3:
    BTB1 G 8 A_FaceTarget
    BTB1 G 0 A_FaceTarget
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlayWeaponSound("weapons/hrfire")
    BTB1 F 4 Bright A_CustomMissile("FasterNewPlasmaBall",32,0,0)
    BTB1 G 0 A_FaceTarget
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlayWeaponSound("weapons/hrfire")
    BTB1 F 4 Bright A_CustomMissile("FasterNewPlasmaBall",32,0,0)
    BTB1 G 0 A_FaceTarget
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlayWeaponSound("weapons/hrfire")
    BTB1 F 4 Bright A_CustomMissile("FasterNewPlasmaBall",32,0,0)
    BTB1 G 0 A_FaceTarget
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlayWeaponSound("weapons/hrfire")
    BTB1 F 4 Bright A_CustomMissile("FasterNewPlasmaBall",32,0,0)
    BTB1 G 0 A_FaceTarget
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlayWeaponSound("weapons/hrfire")
    BTB1 F 4 Bright A_CustomMissile("FasterNewPlasmaBall",32,0,0)
    BTB1 G 0 A_FaceTarget
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlayWeaponSound("weapons/hrfire")
    BTB1 F 3 Bright A_CustomMissile("FasterNewPlasmaBall",32,0,0)
    BTB1 F 1 Bright A_Jump(86,"Missile4")
    Goto See
  Missile4:

    BTB1 G 0 A_FaceTarget
    BTB1 F 4 Bright A_CustomMissile("PlasmaReapShot",32,0,random(-3,3))
    BTB1 G 0 A_FaceTarget
    BTB1 F 4 Bright A_CustomMissile("PlasmaReapShot",32,0,random(-3,3))
    BTB1 G 0 A_FaceTarget
    BTB1 F 4 Bright A_CustomMissile("PlasmaReapShot",32,0,random(-3,3))
	BTB1 G 0 A_FaceTarget
    BTB1 F 4 Bright A_CustomMissile("PlasmaReapShot",32,0,random(-3,3))
    BTB1 G 0 A_FaceTarget
    BTB1 F 4 Bright A_CustomMissile("PlasmaReapShot",32,0,random(-3,3))

ACTOR AssaultConquerorBot : MilitaryEnforcerBot
{

{
  Spawn:

    TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_slot",1)
    SCBT A 10 A_Look
    Goto Idle
  GiveUp:
    SCBT A 35 A_ClearTarget
	Goto Idle
  Idle:

	TNT1 A 0 A_LookEx(LOF_NOSOUNDCHECK)

    Loop
  Find:

    Goto Idle
  See:

    TNT1 A 0 ACS_ExecuteAlways(3601,0,0,0,0)
    TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_script",1)

    TNT1 AAAAAAAAAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UtilityActorSlot",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)

    TNT1 A 0 HealThing(20)
    TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("monsters/clhoof")
    SCBT BCDE 3 A_Chase
    TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("monsters/clhoof")
    TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Check For Master Player Calling Help",0,0,0,0)
    SCBT FGHI 3 A_Chase
    Loop
  Missile:
	SCBT R 5 A_FaceTarget
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("TripleMinigun/Motor",7)
	SCBT RRR 5 A_FaceTarget
	TNT1 A 0 A_StopSound(7)
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("TripleMinigun/FireLoop",CHAN_WEAPON,1,1)
  MissileGo:

    SCBT S 1 Bright A_CustomBulletAttack(5,4,3,random(7,10),"MarineBulletPuff")
	TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget
	TNT1 AA 0 A_CustomMissile("Tracer",70,-12,random(6,-6))
	TNT1 AAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RifleCasing",10,-12,70,-12,random(-2,2),random(0,4),random(-55,-80),SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)

    Goto MissileGo
  Done:
	SCBT R 0 A_PlaySound("TripleMinigun/FireDecay",CHAN_WEAPON,1,0)
	SCBT R 2 A_StopSound(6)
	SCBT RRRRR 2
	SCBT R 2 A_StopSound(7)
	Goto See

    Goto Missile 
  Death:
	TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 A_ScreamAndUnblock
	TNT1 A 0 A_KillChildren
	TNT1 A 0 A_StopSound(6)
	TNT1 A 0 A_StopSound(7)
    SCBT VVVVVVV 2 Bright A_SpawnItemEx("NewKaboomEffect",random(-64,64),random(-64,64),random(12,96))
    SCBT WWWWWWW 2 Bright A_SpawnItemEx("NewKaboomEffect",random(-64,64),random(-64,64),random(12,96))

{

{
     Spawn:
		PLAY A 4 A_Look
		Goto See
	 See:
		PLAY A 0 A_JumpIf(user_nomaster == 1,"Search")
		PLAY A 0 ACS_ExecuteAlways(8883,0,0,0,0)
		PLAY A 0 A_JumpIfTracerCloser(100,"Protect")
		PLAY A 0 A_GiveInventory("AIFollowing",1)
		PLAY A 4 A_Chase("","Missile",CHF_DONTMOVE)
		PLAY A 0 A_JumpIfTracerCloser(150,"Protect")
		PLAY A 0 A_JumpIf(velx != 0 || vely != 0,2)
		PLAY A 0 A_Jump(256,"Search")
		PLAY A 0 A_GiveInventory("AIFollowing",1)
		PLAY B 4 A_Chase("","Missile",CHF_DONTMOVE)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("FootStep",0,0,0,0)
		PLAY A 0 A_JumpIfTracerCloser(150,"Protect")
		PLAY A 0 A_GiveInventory("AIFollowing",1)
		PLAY C 4 A_Chase("","Missile",CHF_DONTMOVE)
		PLAY A 0 A_JumpIfTracerCloser(150,"Protect")
		PLAY A 0 A_GiveInventory("AIFollowing",1)
		PLAY D 4 A_Chase("","Missile",CHF_DONTMOVE)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("FootStep",0,0,0,0)
		Loop
	Protect:
		PLAY E 0 A_ClearTarget
		PLAY E 0 A_SetAngle(random(0,359))
		PLAY E 0 HealThing(1)
		PLAY E 4 A_Chase("","Missile",CHF_DONTMOVE)

		Goto See
		PLAY E 1 A_Jump(8,"Protect")
		Goto Protect+2
    Search:
		PLAY A 0 A_Jump(32,"Find")
		PLAY ABCDABCDABCDABCD 2 A_Chase
		Goto See
	Find:
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_ExecuteAlways(8883,0,0,0,0)
		Goto See
    Missile:
		//TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(45,"FragGrenade")
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(750,"Close")
    Far:
        PLAY EE 5 A_GiveInventory("AIFolloingAndAiming",1)
        PLAY E 0 A_GiveInventory("AIFolloingAndAiming",1)
        TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RifleCasing", 12, 6, 30, Random(2, 6), 0, Random(1, 3), Random(-80, -90), 128)
        PLAY F 2 Bright A_CustomBulletAttack(15.4,0,1,5,"MarineBulletPuff")
        PLAY E 2 A_GiveInventory("AIFolloingAndAiming",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RifleCasing", 12, 6, 30, Random(2, 6), 0, Random(1, 3), Random(-80, -90), 128)
        PLAY F 2 Bright A_CustomBulletAttack(15.4,0,1,5,"MarineBulletPuff")
        PLAY E 2 A_GiveInventory("AIFolloingAndAiming",1)
        TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RifleCasing", 12, 6, 30, Random(2, 6), 0, Random(1, 3), Random(-80, -90), 128)
        PLAY F 2 Bright A_CustomBulletAttack(15.4,0,1,5,"MarineBulletPuff")
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(16,"See")
        TNT1 A 0 A_CPosRefire
        PLAY EE 5 A_GiveInventory("AIFolloingAndAiming",1)
        Goto Far+2
    Close:
        PLAY EE 5 A_GiveInventory("AIFolloingAndAiming",1)
        PLAY E 0 A_GiveInventory("AIFolloingAndAiming",1)
        TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RifleCasing", 12, 6, 30, Random(2, 6), 0, Random(1, 3), Random(-80, -90), 128)
        PLAY F 2 Bright A_CustomBulletAttack(22.5,0,1,random(1,5)*3,"MarineBulletPuff")
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(16,"See")
        TNT1 A 0 A_CPosRefire
        PLAY E 3 A_GiveInventory("AIFolloingAndAiming",1)
		Goto Close+2
   FragGrenade:
        PLA1 E 1 A_JumpIfCloser(1000,1)
		Goto Missile
		PLA1 E 0 A_JumpIfCloser(280,"Missile")
        PLA1 E 6 A_GiveInventory("AIFolloingAndAiming",1)
        PLA1 EEE 4 A_GiveInventory("AIFolloingAndAiming",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("AIFolloingAndAiming",1)
        PLA1 E 6 A_CustomMissile("MGrenade",32,0,0,2,10)
		PLA1 E 1
		Goto See
	 Pain:
		PLAY G 3 A_GiveInventory("AIStrafing",1)
		PLAY G 3 A_Pain
		Goto See
	}
}

ACTOR PurifierDrone : ScoutBot
{
Health 300
Radius 10
Height 48
Mass 500
Speed 8
Scale 0.6
Tag "\c[a6]UAC \c[v2]- \c[m3]Purifier Drone\c-"
States
{
  Spawn:
	PUSB B 10 A_Look
	Goto Idle
  See:
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(16,"GiveUp")
	PUSB A 0 A_PlaySound("b1battlebot/step")
    PUSB AAABBB 2 A_Chase
	PUSB C 0 A_PlaySound("b1battlebot/step")
    PUSB CCCDDD 2 A_Chase
	Loop
  Idle:
    TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(48,"Find")
	TNT1 A 0 A_LookEx(LOF_NOSOUNDCHECK)
	PUSB A 0 A_PlaySound("b1battlebot/step")
    PUSB AAABBB 2 A_Wander
	TNT1 A 0 A_LookEx(LOF_NOSOUNDCHECK)
    PUSB C 0 A_PlaySound("b1battlebot/step")
    PUSB CCCDDD 2 A_Wander
	Loop
  GiveUp:
	PUSB B 35 A_ClearTarget
	Goto Idle
  Find:
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_ExecuteAlways(8883,0,0,0,0)
    Goto Idle
  Missile:
	PUSB DD 5 A_FaceTarget
	PUSB E 0 A_PlaySound("drone/fire")
	PUSB EEEE 1 A_CustomMissile("ErasusSmallProj",24,0,0)
	PUSB E 0 A_CposRefire
	PUSB E 0 A_Jump(32,1)
	Goto Missile+2
  Missileend:
	PUSB DD 5 A_FaceTarget
    Goto Missile+2
  Death:
	PUSB F 0 A_Scream
	PUSB F 0 A_NoBlocking
    PUSB F 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Debris",0,0,0,Random(4,-4),Random(4,-4),Random(4,8),0,128)
	PUSB FFFF 7 Bright  A_CustomMissile("Kaboom", 0, 0, random(0,360), 2, random(0,360))
	PUSB G 250
	Stop
	}
}

    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("MarineBeaconSpawners",-32,32,0,0,0,0,0,32|SXF_SETMASTER)
    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("MarineBeaconSpawners",32,-32,0,0,0,0,0,32|SXF_SETMASTER)
    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("MarineBeaconSpawners",-32,-32,0,0,0,0,0,32|SXF_SETMASTER)
    TNT1 A 0 
  Idle:
    DGIZ A 2 A_SpawnItemEx("UACCommandPostHolo2",0,0,48)
    TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_delay >= 2160,"Done")
	TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_delay",user_delay+1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(1,"UACMarine")
	TNT1 A 0
    Loop
  Done:
    DGIZ AAA 35 A_PlaySound("sentry/warn")
	DGIZ A 1 A_Die
    Goto See
  UACMarine:
    TNT1 A 0
    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("MarineBeaconSpawners",random(-32,32),random(-32,32),0,0,0,0,0,32|SXF_SETMASTER)
    Goto Idle
  Death:
    TNT1 A 0
    TNT1 A 0 A_KillChildren
	DGIZ AAAAAA 2 A_CustomMissile("Kaboom",random(8,80),random(20,-20),random(0,360),2,random(0,360))
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("SmallVehicleExplosionEffect")
    TNT1 A 0 A_NoBlocking
    TNT1 A 0 A_Scream
    DGIZ Z 250
    Stop
  }
}

ACTOR SummonRuneMinion : UACStrongMarine
{
Monster
Health 500
Radius 9
Height 56
Speed 15

MaxStepHeight 32

DamageFactor "Marine", 0
DamageFactor "MarinePierce", 0.0
DamageFactor "MarineKaboom", 0.0
DamageFactor "Legendary", 0
DamageFactor "LegendaryGuruPlayer", 0
DamageFactor "LegendaryGuru", 0
DamageFactor "MechStep", 0
DamageFactor "Mine", 0
DamageFactor "DBFG2", 0
RadiusDamageFactor 0.75
DamageFactor 0.75
SeeSound "minion/see"
PainSound "minion/pain"
DeathSound "minion/death"
ActiveSound "minion/idle"
MinMissileChance 2
+NODROPOFF
+FRIENDLY
+QUICKTORETALIATE
+DONTHARMSPECIES
+MISSILEMORE
+MISSILEEVENMORE
+NOBLOCKMONST
+FLOORCLIP
+NOPAIN
//-SOLID

var int user_follow;

Tag "\c[D4]Summoner Rune \c[S7]Death Knight\c-"
States
{
  Spawn:
	DKNT A 4 A_Look
	Goto See
  See:
	DKNT P 0 A_JumpIf(user_nomaster == 1,"Search")
	DKNT P 0 ACS_ExecuteAlways(8883,0,0,0,0)
	DKNT P 0 A_JumpIfTracerCloser(100,"Protect")
	DKNT P 0 A_GiveInventory("AIFollowing",1)
	DKNT P 4 A_Chase("","Missile",CHF_DONTMOVE)
	DKNT Q 0 HealThing(2)
	DKNT Q 0 A_JumpIfTracerCloser(150,"Protect")
	DKNT Q 0 A_JumpIf(velx != 0 || vely != 0,2)
	DKNT Q 0 A_Jump(256,"Search")
	DKNT Q 0 A_GiveInventory("AIFollowing",1)
	DKNT Q 4 A_Chase("","Missile",CHF_DONTMOVE)
	DKNT R 0 A_SpawnItem("BonyStep",0,0,0,0)
	DKNT R 0 A_JumpIfTracerCloser(150,"Protect")
	DKNT R 0 A_GiveInventory("AIFollowing",1)
	DKNT R 0 A_JumpIfInventory("HasSummonerRune",1,2,AAPTR_TRACER)
	DKNT R 0 A_Die
	DKNT R 4 A_Chase("","Missile",CHF_DONTMOVE)
	DKNT S 0 A_JumpIfTracerCloser(150,"Protect")
	DKNT S 0 A_GiveInventory("AIFollowing",1)
	DKNT S 4 A_Chase("","Missile",CHF_DONTMOVE)
	DKNT S 0 A_SpawnItem("BonyStep",0,0,0,0)
	Loop
  Protect:
	//DKNT T 0 A_Stop
	DKNT T 0 A_ClearTarget

	DKNT T 4 A_Chase("","Missile",CHF_DONTMOVE)
	DKNT T 4 A_JumpIfTracerCloser(200,1)
	Goto See
	DKNT T 1 A_Jump(8,"Protect")
	Goto Protect+2
  Search:
	DKNT A 0 A_Jump(32,"Find")
	DKNT A 0 A_SpawnItem("BonyStep",0,0,0,0)
	DKNT AAABBB 2 A_Chase
	DKNT A 0 A_SpawnItem("BonyStep",0,0,0,0)

	TNT1 A 0 ACS_ExecuteAlways(8883,0,0,0,0)
	Goto See

	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(88,"HeadShot")
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(88,"BoltShot")
  Normal:

	DKNT G 0 A_CustomMissile("SRMDart",32,0,1,0)
	DKNT G 6 Bright A_CustomMissile("SRMDart",32,0,3,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,"HeadShot")

	DISC A 1 A_Jump(8,"Protect")
	Goto Protect+3
  Search:
	DISC A 0 A_Jump(32,"Find")
	DISC AAABBBAAABBB 2 A_Chase
	Goto See
  Find:
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_ExecuteAlways(8883,0,0,0,0)
	Goto See
  Missile:
	TNT1 A 0 
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("MinionDisciple/See")
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,"WindSlicer","StormLite","FireTracer","IceBeam")
  WindSlicer:
	DISC CCCCCCCCC 3 Bright A_GiveInventory("AIFolloingAndAiming",1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_wait",0)
  WindSlicerGo:
    TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_wait >= 9,"See")	 
    TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_wait",user_wait+1)
	DISC D 0 A_CustomMissile("PAvatarWindSlicer",36,0,random(-5,5))
	DISC DD 3 Bright A_GiveInventory("AIFolloingAndAiming",1)
	Loop
  StormLite:
	DISC EEEEEEEEE 3 Bright A_GiveInventory("AIFolloingAndAiming",1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_wait",0)
  StormLiteGo:
    TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_wait >= 24,"See")	 
    TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_wait",user_wait+1)
	DISC F 0 A_PlayWeaponSound("legbanished/attack2")
	DISC F 0 A_CustomMissile("MAvatarStormLite",36,0,0)
	DISC F 2 Bright A_GiveInventory("AIFolloingAndAiming",1)
	Loop
  FireTracer:
	DISC SSSSSSSSS 3 Bright A_GiveInventory("AIFolloingAndAiming",1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_wait",0)
  FireTracerGo:
    TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_wait >= 28,"See")	 
    TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_wait",user_wait+1)
	DISC T 0 A_CustomMissile("PAvatarFireTracer",36,0,0)
	DISC T 2 Bright A_GiveInventory("AIFolloingAndAiming",1)
	Loop
  IceBeam:
	DISC QQQQQQQQQ 3 Bright A_GiveInventory("AIFolloingAndAiming",1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_wait",0)
  IceBeamGo:
    TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_wait >= 38,"See")	 
    TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_wait",user_wait+1)
	DISC R 0 A_CustomMissile("MAvatarIceBeam",36,0,0)
	DISC R 2 Bright A_GiveInventory("AIFolloingAndAiming",1)
	Loop
  XDeath:
  Death: 
	DISC HHHH 2 Bright A_CustomMissile("AvatarIceChargeEffect",random(8,72),random(16,-16),random(0,360),2,random(0,360))
	DISC HHHH 2 Bright A_CustomMissile("CardinalFire",random(8,72),random(16,-16),random(0,360),2,random(0,360))
	DISC HHHH 2 Bright A_CustomMissile("WhiteStar",random(8,72),random(16,-16),random(0,360),2,random(0,360))
	DISC HHHH 2 Bright A_CustomMissile("AvatarRedKaboom",random(8,72),random(16,-16),random(0,360),2,random(0,360))
	DISC I 5 Bright A_Scream
	DISC J 5 Bright
	DISC K 5 Bright A_NoBlocking 
	DISC LMN 4 Bright  
	DISC O 250
	Stop 
}
